--
-- Table structure for table `log_surveys`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `log_surveys`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `log_surveys` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `originalId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `programId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `status` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'1',
  `requireEngagement` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'1',
  `allowEngagement` bit(1) DEFAULT b'1',
  `duplicatesAllowed` bit(1) DEFAULT b'1',
  `title` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `doneButtonText` varchar(30) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Done',
  `doneBtnActivityCodeId` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `nextButtonText` varchar(30) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Next',
  `prevButtonText` varchar(30) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Prev',
  `reminderStatus` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `reminderText` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `dateModified` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `dateInserted` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `triggerType` varchar(1) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `nextBtnActivityCodeId` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `prevBtnActivityCodeId` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `surveyId_idx` (`id`),
  KEY `programId_idx` (`programId`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=22 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;

CREATE TABLE `programPatients` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `programId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `systemUserId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `MCIReview` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `status` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'1',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `patientId_idx` (`id`),
  KEY `programId_idx` (`programId`),
  KEY `fk_programPatients_staffMemberId` (`systemUserId`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_programPatients_programId` FOREIGN KEY (`programId`) REFERENCES `programs` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_programPatients_staffMemberId` FOREIGN KEY (`systemUserId`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=8 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

--
-- Table structure for table `storage_patients`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `storage_patients`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `storage_patients` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'primary key for patient, it will serve as our system''s patient Id',
  `programpatientId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sourcePatientId` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id assigned to patient by source system - e.g Pat148R-2KD-BOS',
  `prefix` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Mr, Dr., Ms, Sir, Princess, Knight, etc',
  `firstName` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. John',
  `middleName` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g Joshua',
  `lastName` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Doe',
  `suffix` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Jr, III, IV etc.',
  `dob` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Patient''s date of birth 1-1-1912',
  `genderId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Look up value from lu_Genders. Look up field is int and not free hand field because we should have some limits to some fields as what the user can type.  We will add it to our look up table if something creative comes up.  It is also a repetitive field, using int will take up less space and faster when it comes to indexing\nSample equivalent values are - male, female, unknown, transgender, etc.',
  `raceId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Look up Id from lu_Races - equivalent values could be Asian, White, Black, etc.',
  `hispanicId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_Hispanics\nSample look up values are Yes, No, Not Reported',
  `primaryLanguageId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id from lu_Languages - Sample look up values - English, Spanish, Polish, Mandarin (Chinese), Cantonese (Chinese) etc.',
  `englishProficient` varchar(10) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'can be Yes, No, Unknown...\nWe wi\nso changing it to varchar',
  `maritalStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'look up from lu_MartialStatuses - Sample look up values are - Single, Married, Divorced, Not Reported, etc.',
  `email` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. test@test.com',
  `additionalContactNumber` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `url` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. http://test.com',
  `occupation` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `guardianName` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'name of guardian - Jane Doe, John Smith',
  `emergencyContact` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Name of emergency contact - Jane Doe',
  `emergencyTel` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '123-456-7890',
  `patientStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_PatientStatuses - Could be equivalent int value of active, pending, future, expired, etc.',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',
  `race` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `lastContacted` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `clientType` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `genderFK_idx` (`genderId`),
  KEY `raceFK_idx` (`raceId`),
  KEY `lauguageFK_idx` (`primaryLanguageId`),
  KEY `martialStatusFK_idx` (`maritalStatusId`),
  KEY `hispanicFK_idx` (`hispanicId`),
  KEY `patientFK_idx` (`programpatientId`),
  CONSTRAINT `genderFK` FOREIGN KEY (`genderId`) REFERENCES `lu_genders` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `hispanicFK` FOREIGN KEY (`hispanicId`) REFERENCES `lu_hispanics` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `lauguageFK` FOREIGN KEY (`primaryLanguageId`) REFERENCES `lu_languages` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `martialStatusFK` FOREIGN KEY (`maritalStatusId`) REFERENCES `lu_maritalStatuses` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `patientFK` FOREIGN KEY (`programpatientId`) REFERENCES `programPatients` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `raceFK` FOREIGN KEY (`raceId`) REFERENCES `lu_races` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=8 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

CREATE TABLE `survey_questions` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `surveyId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `surveyPageId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `hide` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `required` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `requiredResponse` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'This question requires an answer.',
  `dspQuestionId` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `question` text COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `answerTypeId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `columnsDisplayed` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `allowMultipleAns` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `saveToFieldId` int(11) DEFAULT '0',
  `autoPopulateFromField` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `questionNum` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `validationId` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `alphabeticallySort` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'0',
  `choiceLayout` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `populateFromTable` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted` bit(1) DEFAULT b'0',
  `otherOption` bit(1) DEFAULT b'0',
  `otherLabel` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `otherDspChoice` int(11) DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0 = Empty\n1 = Display as answer choice\n2 = Display as comment field',
  `dateFormatType` int(11) DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0 = empty\n1 = MM / DD / YYYY\n2 = DD/ MM / YYYY',
  `collectDateInfo` bit(1) DEFAULT b'0',
  `collectTimeInfo` bit(1) DEFAULT b'0',
  `dateDspType` int(11) DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '1 = Below\n2 = Side by Side',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `pageId_idx` (`surveyPageId`),
  KEY `sq_ansType` (`answerTypeId`),
  CONSTRAINT `sq_ansType` FOREIGN KEY (`answerTypeId`) REFERENCES `lu_answerTypes` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `sq_sp` FOREIGN KEY (`surveyPageId`) REFERENCES `survey_pages` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=51 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `systemUserId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `patientId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `activityCodeId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `activityCodeDesc` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `callDate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `userId_idx` (`systemUserId`),
  KEY `fk_usersSchedule_patientId` (`patientId`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_usersSchedule_patientId` FOREIGN KEY (`patientId`) REFERENCES `programPatients` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_usersSchedule_userid` FOREIGN KEY (`systemUserId`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

  `typeId` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `roleId` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '2',
  `status` bit(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT b'1',
  `firstName` varchar(55) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `lastName` varchar(55) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `createdBy` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',

  `resetCode` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `randomSalt` blob,
  `encryptedPw` blob,
  `lastloggedIn` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `userRoleId_idx` (`roleId`),

  CONSTRAINT `userRoleId` FOREIGN KEY (`roleId`) REFERENCES `user_roles` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=17 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `insertValidationErrors` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `insertValidationErrors`(in vtType int, in dspPos int, in fieldId int,
in programUploadId int, in programUploadRecordId int)
BEGIN

DECLARE regEx varchar(100) DEFAULT '';
DECLARE errorId int DEFAULT 0;


CASE vtType
	WHEN 2 THEN 
		BEGIN set regEx = '^[A-Z0-9._%-]+@[A-Z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z]{2,4}$';
        set errorId = 2;
        END;
    WHEN 3 THEN 
		BEGIN 
			CALL `rapidregistry`.`stripPhoneChars`(vtType, dspPos, programUploadId,  programUploadRecordId);
			set regEx ='^[0-9]{7,11}$';
            set errorId = 28;
		END;
	WHEN 5 THEN BEGIN
		set regEx = '^-?[0-9]+[.]?[0-9]*$|^-?[.][0-9]+$';
        set errorId = 30;
        END;
    ELSE
        BEGIN
        END;
	END 
	CASE;

IF (programUploadRecordId = 0) THEN
set @stmt = concat(
'insert into programUpload_Errors (programUploadId, programUploadRecordId, dspPos, fieldId, errorid, errorData) 
SELECT ', programUploadId, ', programUploadRecordId, ',dspPos,',' , fieldId, ', ' , errorId, ', F',  dspPos, 
' FROM programUploadRecordDetails WHERE trim(F' ,dspPos, ') not REGEXP  "', regEx, '" and F',dspPos, ' is not null 
and length(F', dspPos, ') != 0
and length(trim(F', dspPos, ')) != 0
and length(REPLACE(REPLACE(F', dspPos,' , "\n", ""), "\r", "") != 0)  and programUploadRecordId 
in (select id from programUploadRecords where programUploadId = ', programUploadId,' and statusId not in (11,12,13,16));'
);

BEGIN -- true
		PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
		EXECUTE stmt;
END; 
END IF;

IF (programUploadRecordId != 0) THEN

set @stmt= concat(
'insert into programUpload_Errors (programUploadId, programUploadRecordId, dspPos,  fieldId, errorid, errorData) 
SELECT ', programUploadId, ', programUploadRecordId, ',dspPos, ',', fieldId,',', errorId, ', F',dspPos, 
' FROM programUploadRecordDetails WHERE trim(F' ,dspPos, ') not REGEXP  "', regEx, '" and F',dspPos, ' is not null 
and length(F', dspPos, ') != 0
and length(trim(F', dspPos, ')) != 0
and length(REPLACE(REPLACE(F', dspPos,', "\n", ""), "\r", "") != 0) and programUploadRecordId = ', 
programUploadRecordId);

BEGIN -- true
		PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
		EXECUTE stmt;


END; 
END IF;


END ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;
/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `stripPhoneChars` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `stripPhoneChars`(in vtType int, in dspPos int,
in programUploadId int, in programUploadRecordId int)
BEGIN

	DECLARE varToReplace varchar(100) DEFAULT '.';
	DECLARE part1 varchar(255) DEFAULT '.';
	DECLARE part2 varchar(25) DEFAULT '.';
	
	if (programUploadRecordId = 0) then
	BEGIN
		set part1 = concat("update programUploadRecordDetails JOIN (SELECT id from programUploadRecords WHERE programUploadId = ", programUploadId, 
        " and statusId not in (11,12,13,16)) as ti ON programUploadRecordDetails.programUploadRecordId = ti.id SET programUploadRecordDetails.F"
	  , dspPos, " = replace(F", dspPos, ", '");
	END;
	END if;

	if (programUploadRecordId != 0) then
	BEGIN
	  set part1 = concat("update programUploadRecordDetails JOIN (SELECT id from programUploadRecords WHERE id = ",
	  programUploadRecordId, ") as ti ON programUploadRecordDetails.programUploadRecordId = ti.id SET programUploadRecordDetails.F"
	  , dspPos, " = replace(F", dspPos, ", '");
	END;
	END if;

	
	set part2 = "', '');";
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
  	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = '-';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = ')';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = '(';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = ' ';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

 END ;;
DELIMITER ;
